***изрыгать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изрыгать.html>изрыга́ть</a> (22339)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">изры́гнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izrýgnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изрыгать.html>изрыга́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izrygátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изры́гнуть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to belch, to disgorge, to spew out
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1998</b>,  Александр Суханов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Sukhanov" class="extiw" title="w:Alexander Sukhanov">Alexander Sukhanov</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:дракон.html>Драко́н</a></cite>  | <cite>Dragon playing the violin</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>Моя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорогой.html>дорога́я</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:изрыгать.html>изрыга́я</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дракон.html>драко́н</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́н</a>...</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I skazál on: Moja dorogája, ne mogú ja, ogónʹ <b>izrygája</b>, v bášne žitʹ kak drakón, što za glúpyj zakón...</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And he said: My dear, as I belch fire, I cannot live in a tower, what a silly regulation...</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ры<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***изувеченный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изувеченный.html>изуве́ченный</a> (16467)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***изумить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изумить.html>изуми́ть</a> (26737)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изумить.html>изуми́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izumítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изумлять.html>изумля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to amaze, to astound, to astonish, to strike <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to fill with surprise</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уродовать.html>уро́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uródovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изуродовать.html>изуро́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izuródovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уродовать.html>уро́довать</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изучить.html>изучи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изучать.html>изуча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izučátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изучить.html>изучи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to study, to learn <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">implying that an individual or a group is studying or learning something with an in-depth approach</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<li>to scrutinize</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jézditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изъездить.html>изъе́здить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izʺjézditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изъезжа́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go, to travel all over</li>
<li>to ruin (e.g. a road) by riding on for too long</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
